Top 32 Decklists
================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX SINGAPORE 2015](/en/events/coverage/gpsin15)
 on June 28, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast











With the "trilogy" coming to an end (Charlotte, Copenhagen, and Singapore), we know some of you are still in the mood for more Modern! Let us continue to whet your appetite with the Top 32 decklists of Grand Prix Singapore as we welcome the arrival of *Magic Origins*!
